        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1209714272" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16709757417202235506"><b>☆☆5++++++ Creed & Sylvie Stars!☆☆☆</b><br/><br/>First off, even though this is only my 3rd KA read, this is my favorite couple! This was just wow! There's a ton of reviews on this already so I'll just express my thoughts and feelings. So forgive me in advance for all the blabbering. <br/><br/>Sylvie is in my top 5 favorite heriones! This was one bad chick! She was rough, raw, real, dirty-talking, could hang with the guys, sort of gal. She was definitely an alpha-female, a lioness. And I loved her. Life made her rough, </span>
  <span id="freeText16709757417202235506" style="display:none"><b>☆☆5++++++ Creed &amp; Sylvie Stars!☆☆☆</b><br><br>First off, even though this is only my 3rd KA read, this is my favorite couple! This was just wow! There's a ton of reviews on this already so I'll just express my thoughts and feelings. So forgive me in advance for all the blabbering. <br><br>Sylvie is in my top 5 favorite heriones! This was one bad chick! She was rough, raw, real, dirty-talking, could hang with the guys, sort of gal. She was definitely an alpha-female, a lioness. And I loved her. Life made her rough, but I love how through the story she softens up and allows love into her life. <br><br>This story was so raw and edgy. Sylvie and Creed loved each other from a young age, but horrible circumstances pulled them apart for 16 years! And yet their love never fizzled.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425066582ra/13840026.gif" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This story touched my heart in ways I didn't think possible. The characters were all so solid and well rounded. I loved how Knight was apart of the story. And Creed...what can I say about Creed except he was amazing!!! He's my book-husband. He loved Sylvie with a consuming, passionate love and his devotion to her was beyond incredible. Words can't describe this alpha. He makes my heart go a-flutter.<br><br>I don't know how KA does it, but she writes a mean epilogue! I was like this at the end of it:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425066356ra/13839985.gif" width="400" height="320" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If I had to describe this story it would be this: <i>Love can stand the test of time.</i> Yes it's raw, dirty, grimy, sad, and I can see why this story would rub some people the wrong way, but it's real and all I can say is I LOVE, LOVE LOVED it!</span>
  <a data-text-id="16709757417202235506" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_332336317" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/332336317" />
    <a title="❤️ Dorsey aka Wrath Lover Reviews ❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5205999-dorsey-aka-wrath-lover-reviews"><img alt="❤️ Dorsey aka Wrath Lover Reviews ❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1485279859p2/5205999.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/332336317?book_show_action=true">May 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="❤️ Dorsey aka Wrath Lover Reviews ❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="❤️ Dorsey aka Wrath Lover Reviews ❤️" href="/user/show/5205999-dorsey-aka-wrath-lover-reviews">❤️ Dorsey aka Wrath Lover Reviews ❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5205999-dorsey-aka-wrath-lover-reviews?shelf=audio_books">audio_books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5205999-dorsey-aka-wrath-lover-reviews?shelf=kristen_ashley">kristen_ashley</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer332336317" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3515957173274006856"><br/><br/><a href='http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/Book%20Review%20Photos/11575720_zpsb424590b.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417728809i/12513177.jpg' alt=' photo 11575720_zpsb424590b.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>* I never got around to writing a review for <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13640229.Creed__Unfinished_Hero___2_' title='Creed (Unfinished Hero, #2) by Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Creed</a> after reading the book, so with the newly released audio book, I've decided to do an Audio Book Review. <br/><br/><b>
  <i> 5 "Beautiful Love" Stars!!!”</i>
</b> <br/><br/>Sylvie Bissenette is a badass alpha female who carries a gun, talks trash and kicks ass. Sylvie works for Knight protecting the girls in his stable. She's also a PI who on occasion works with Hawk Delgado & Lee Nightingale. She keeps her life private and has only ever loved one man, Tucker Creed and she ha</span>
  <span id="freeText3515957173274006856" style="display:none"><br><br><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/Book%20Review%20Photos/11575720_zpsb424590b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417728809i/12513177.jpg" alt=" photo 11575720_zpsb424590b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>* I never got around to writing a review for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13640229.Creed__Unfinished_Hero___2_" title="Creed (Unfinished Hero, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Creed</a> after reading the book, so with the newly released audio book, I've decided to do an Audio Book Review. <br><br><b>
  <i> 5 "Beautiful Love" Stars!!!”</i>
</b> <br><br>Sylvie Bissenette is a badass alpha female who carries a gun, talks trash and kicks ass. Sylvie works for Knight protecting the girls in his stable. She's also a PI who on occasion works with Hawk Delgado &amp; Lee Nightingale. She keeps her life private and has only ever loved one man, Tucker Creed and she has loved him since she was 6 yrs old.<br><br>Sylvie met Tucker Creed when she was six years old, she would run into the woods with her constant companion (her dog Bootsie), she would run away from the ugliness at home. On one of her nighttime escapes she runs into eleven year old Tucker Creed whose home is just as ugly, they become friends and each others safe haven when Tucker tells Sylvie that they will take care of each other when the ugliness comes.<br><br>Later as they get older, They meet at the pier which becomes “their” special meeting place. It’s a safe place where they can do cannonballs, talk, swim, and eat frozen snickers bars. Eventually the fondness they have for one another turns into love and continues to grow with each year that passes. Until her 18th birthday when he vanishes....and it will be 16 years before she see's him again.<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Come back to me,” I begged, the tear slipping over my eye and gliding down my cheek.” - Sylvie (waiting for Tucker at their pier)</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/Book%20Review%20Photos/PicsArt_1429342066759_zpsosrqafiu.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429342215i/14575097.jpg" alt=" photo PicsArt_1429342066759_zpsosrqafiu.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The amount of cruelness (Tucker) Creed &amp; Sylvie suffered and what was taken from them in the most heinous way was devastating. The story of their past and the mystery that kept them apart is revealed throughout the book. Creed and Sylvie share what they’ve been through, some revealed during conversations, some through flashbacks, and some through Sylvie’s hellish nightmares. <br><br>There were a couple of things that bothered me, like the fact that Creed never checked up on Sylvie, it was later explained and made complete sense but I still found it hard to get past. Creed moved on with his life, he married, he created a family, and eventually divorced because he was never in love with anyone other than Sylvie. There is more to that story but you'll need to read about it and form your own opinions.<br><br>Knight has a pretty substantial role in Sylvie's life, his relationship with Sylvie was amazingly heartwarming, and I loved seeing what the two of them shared. We also get to meet Creed’s family and as always with KA, she brings them all together beautifully. <br><br><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/Book%20Review%20Photos/PicsArt_1429341588563_zps036a2utl.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429342308i/14575101.jpg" alt=" photo PicsArt_1429341588563_zps036a2utl.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>A Few Of My Favorite Quotes:<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“We've been through a lot and you've earned a piece of my heart, babe. It’s all yours and always will be.”- Knight to Sylvie”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Sylvie,” he called and I whirled and snapped, “What?” “Bottom of my soul,” he whispered across the room, eyes locked to mine. I sucked in breath through my nose before I whispered back, “Bottom of mine."- Knight to Sylvie””</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote> “Born to love you, baby,” he repeated. “Die lovin’ you, my Sylvie””</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote> “You love me?” he asked quietly. I dipped my face close and answered quietly, “On a cold night, a long time ago, you put your hands almost exactly where they are right now and, I might have been six years old, but I fell hard. So, yeah. For over twenty-seven years, every day, every minute, every second, I’ve loved you, Tucker Creed.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br><br><br><u>Playlist:</u><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://youtu.be/A7tEx8bMBk0">http://youtu.be/A7tEx8bMBk0</a> - Remember When by Carrie Underwood<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://youtu.be/LgCWgfwlk0M">http://youtu.be/LgCWgfwlk0M</a> - DreamWeaver by Gary Wright<br><br><br>* The audio book is just as great as the book. Creed is narrated by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/8063470.MacKenzie_Cartwright" title="MacKenzie Cartwright" rel="nofollow noopener">MacKenzie Cartwright</a> who does a fantastic job!!<br><br><br>Originally Read: September 2012</span>
  <a data-text-id="3515957173274006856" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16028155-creed">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of KA; fans of angsty, contemporary/erotic romance</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=for_my_kindle">for_my_kindle</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer553080572" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5152257102113902768">Oh the <i>angst</i>! Oh the <i>anguish</i>! Oh the <b>sex</b>! (lol) This book had a <i>lot</i> of it all.<br/><br/> This one was a little different than the usual KA, because basically the plot was about longtime friends/lovers Sylvie (34) and Creed (39) finding their way back to each other after 16 painful years apart...and there really wasn't much else going on. A mildly suspenseful plot that had Sylvie and Creed both working together (they're both PI's) for Knight really just sort of fizzled and had some loose ends. While I did </span>
  <span id="freeText5152257102113902768" style="display:none">Oh the <i>angst</i>! Oh the <i>anguish</i>! Oh the <b>sex</b>! (lol) This book had a <i>lot</i> of it all.<br><br> This one was a little different than the usual KA, because basically the plot was about longtime friends/lovers Sylvie (34) and Creed (39) finding their way back to each other after 16 painful years apart...and there really wasn't much else going on. A mildly suspenseful plot that had Sylvie and Creed both working together (they're both PI's) for Knight really just sort of fizzled and had some loose ends. While I did enjoy Creed immediately (c'mon, who wouldn't!), it took me a little time to fall for the adult Sylvie--her badassness took some getting used to at first. But I did eventually enjoy her and respect her.<br><br><i>Creed...</i><br> <a href="http://s880.beta.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/books/43b4c1bf-f58d-48ad-9e76-7355184a1049_zps3aa81b48.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380412194i/810517.jpg" alt=" photo 43b4c1bf-f58d-48ad-9e76-7355184a1049_zps3aa81b48.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>The book didn't flow so smoothly for me. And I hate to admit it, but half way through I found myself wondering "is anything going to happen in this book--they seem happy--now what?" It was hard to keep reading from the present day and then jumping back in time while KA <i>eventually</i> led you to read what happened to cause the breakup of their relationship. It was sad and horribly painful (those no good parents!) but I felt a little bit was missing. I wanted to <i>read</i> a little bit about what happened when <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Sylvie was sold off to that no good pimp/drug dealer, rather than being <i>told</i> what happened. I think that would've made even more of an impact. I wanted to read what Creed did when he finally escaped from Sylvie's rotten father. Did he ever try to look for her? Or did he believe that 'promise' he made? And why didn't he look for her years later, if he was so obsessed? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Those questions kind of bugged me.<br><br><i>Sylvie and Creed</i>...<br><a href="http://s880.beta.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/books/d6cf2cea-e5d1-4558-8095-d3f6d050192e_zps5c90b288.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380412194i/810518.jpg" alt=" photo d6cf2cea-e5d1-4558-8095-d3f6d050192e_zps5c90b288.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I did enjoy seeing Knight(!) and Anya again, liked the relationship between Sylvie and her neighbor Charlene, <i>and</i> Sylvie's relationship with Creed and <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[his kids (what a good dad!) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. And while I thought the sexual relationship between Sylvie and Creed was flamin' <i>hot</i>, dare I say that maybe there was a bit <i>too much</i> of a good thing? When I start thinking "maybe I'll skim over this" that isn't a good sign for me...<br><br><i>They were hot together...</i><br><a href="http://s880.beta.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/books/creedgif_zpsaf3f9eee.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/499135.gif" alt=" photo creedgif_zpsaf3f9eee.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But oh boy, that epilogue? Wow! I wanted a HEA for Creed and Sylvie, and man did KA give them one--and then some!:)<br><br>Not my absolute favorite from this author, but still a must read for her fans. And any potential new fans--this can be read as a stand alone. Enjoy! 4 stars</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1419177234" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1419177234" />
    <a title="NMmomof4" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4"><img alt="NMmomof4" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515474309p2/24665574.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1419177234?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NMmomof4" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NMmomof4" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4">NMmomof4</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=scribd">scribd</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=separation-with-other-partners">separation-with-other-partners</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1419177234" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10517609967380051156"><b> 4 Stars <i>(Originally Read 10/17/2015)</i></b><br/><br/><b> 3.5 Stars <i>(Re-Read 11/4/2019)</i></b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b>I always enjoy <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley' title='Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kristen Ashley</a>, and always have expectations when picking out her books. I expect strong characterization for our main characters, great side character relationships, true love type connections, drama and even suspense at times, and sweet moment that make me happy...and I got all that with this book. As a mom, I also always love when her characters have interactions with kids...so that aspect of th</span>
  <span id="freeText10517609967380051156" style="display:none"><b> 4 Stars <i>(Originally Read 10/17/2015)</i></b><br /><br /><b> 3.5 Stars <i>(Re-Read 11/4/2019)</i></b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b>I always enjoy <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" title="Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a>, and always have expectations when picking out her books. I expect strong characterization for our main characters, great side character relationships, true love type connections, drama and even suspense at times, and sweet moment that make me happy...and I got all that with this book. As a mom, I also always love when her characters have interactions with kids...so that aspect of this book didn't disappoint either. The only reason I have it as a 4 instead of a 5 star read is that the ending seemed a little drawn out. Not the jump ahead epilogue type parts -- but the part before that felt like it could've been edited down to me.<br /><br /><b>*Re-Read Update*:</b> I enjoyed it, but like I said in my original review, it felt too drawn out in the end. It also felt a little too mushy. I still liked it though! ...just probably isn't going to be one of my go-tos for a KA re-read<br /><br /><b>Storyline: </b> This is Sylvie and Creed's story. They meet one night when Sylvie is taking a walk to get away from her Dad fighting with her step mom, and Creed is doing the same with his Mom and her boyfriend. They bond instantly once they realize that they have this big thing in common. They build an amazing connection over the years that just continues to grow. When Sylvie finally turns 18, they have a plan to run away together and start new lives together away from their parents. Only Creed doesn't show up when and where they were supposed to meet. Some other things happen that I don't want to ruin, but we get to the part where they are reunited 16 years later while assigned to partner on a job assigned by Knight (from the first book in the series, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13565914.Knight__Unfinished_Hero___1_" title="Knight (Unfinished Hero, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Knight</a>). There are truths revealed, adjustments to be made, and lots of happy times to make up for...but the couple do all of that and get their HEAs.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This was primarily in Sylvie POV, and Creed's POV for a few sections.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good. KA books always run on the long side, but I never feel it. I always breeze right through. I did have some issues with the ending (before the epilogues) moving along too slow, but I didn't feel the need to skim. No instalove for sure, since they have known each other since Syvie was 6 and Creed was 11, but we do get them 16 years later when the feelings are already developed (but we do get flashbacks to give us the development of those feelings).<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 4 stars. Creed. I liked his ability to put Syvie in her place, but at the same time wait patiently for her to get there. He was really sweet at times, and an overall good man.<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 4 stars. Sylvie. I loved her bad_ss ways, she was extremely loyal, sweet when she needed to be, and I loved her relationship with Knight, and Charlene (and her kids) too.<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b> Moderate. I did tear up a few times, as it covers some heavy themes.<br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Moderate. Typical KA with a good bit of sexy times, but not so much that it takes away from the story.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Rape - mentions of it, domestic abuse - both h and H grew up around it.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b>This had a complete HEA. It didn't have an epilogue per se, but it had many time jumps so we can see their happiness through different milestones and it was sweet.<br /><br /><b>Worth the $?:</b> It was part of my scribed subscription, so yes! But at $3.99 on Amazon, I'd still say yes.</span>

<div id="review_365868947" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/365868947" />
    <a title="KatLynne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2435483-katlynne"><img alt="KatLynne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1296698899p2/2435483.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/365868947?book_show_action=true">Jul 11, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="KatLynne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="KatLynne" href="/user/show/2435483-katlynne">KatLynne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=2012-reads">2012-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=keeper">keeper</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=favorite-treasures">favorite-treasures</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=tattooed-bad-boy-hottie">tattooed-bad-boy-hottie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=hero-favorite-smokin-hot-sexay">hero-favorite-smokin-hot-sexay</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=heroine-i-loved">heroine-i-loved</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=one-of-my-favorite-series">one-of-my-favorite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=heroine-tormented-flawed">heroine-tormented-flawed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=g-contemporary-romance">g-contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=heroine-with-backbone-smart-strong">heroine-with-backbone-smart-strong</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer365868947" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11465665858817425497"><b> “Whatever our souls are made of, his and mine are the same.”…..Emily Bronte</b> <br/><br/><i>Creed</i> is the second installment in Kristen Ashley’s <i>Unfinished Hero</i> Series and a HUGE hit with me! I was enthralled as the story weaves back and forth in time, taking me from present day Colorado back into a small Kentucky town twenty eight years earlier. There I met six year old Sylvie and eleven year old Tucker Creed. Through the hardships of their childhood, a deep abiding friendship blossoms. Creed becomes her prote</span>
  <span id="freeText11465665858817425497" style="display:none"><b> “Whatever our souls are made of, his and mine are the same.”…..Emily Bronte</b> <br /><br /><i>Creed</i> is the second installment in Kristen Ashley’s <i>Unfinished Hero</i> Series and a HUGE hit with me! I was enthralled as the story weaves back and forth in time, taking me from present day Colorado back into a small Kentucky town twenty eight years earlier. There I met six year old Sylvie and eleven year old Tucker Creed. Through the hardships of their childhood, a deep abiding friendship blossoms. Creed becomes her protector and as the years go by this special relationship develops into a beautiful and unwavering love. <br /><br />They both agreed they had to leave this town to escape the monsters that also lived there. For Sylvie, one was called Dad and the other was referred to as stepmonster. Creed had one too, and her name was Mom. <br /><br />So they plotted and planned, excited and looking forward to the day they could launch their future together. All packed, the meeting place and time arranged, the hope in their hearts is palpable. But, Sylvie’s Creed never shows. She's devastated and overcome with shock and grief. The Creed I had come to know would never leave his Sylvie waiting. She was his love, his heart, the very breath he needed to survive.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Born to love you, baby," he repeated. "Die lovin' you, my Sylvie."</i>
</b><br /><br />Tucker Creed aka Creed is much more than another badass, alpha hero. The manner in which the author reveals his layers had me falling for him slowly, bit-by-bit up until my total surrender. <br /><br />The agony of living a life without Sylvie has left a man who merely exists. When circumstances once again change his life drastically, he steps up to the plate to do what is right. Even with the few rays of brightness that have been given back into his life, he’s still empty and loving only one woman.<br /><br />We find Sylvie in Colorado doing work for Knight Sebring. She’s a kick-ass heroine and not the same young, innocent girl Creed knew sixteen years earlier. She takes no crap and is capable of taking care of herself in almost every way. Traumatized by betrayal and living a life of abuse, she’s wrapped herself deep in a protective shell. Shaped by life’s lessons, I understood her reasoning and fears. Her background of horror is overwhelming, leaving in its wake a determination I admired.<br /><br />Kristen Ashley has once again given us a story that drew me in completely. I easily became submerged into the life of this couple. I felt their joy and hope as they made plans for a future together and then the despair and desolation when separated. The hardships they endured as children and the incredible pain they each suffered as adults brought me into their darkness. With everything shattered, we get to see how life has molded each of them. There's also beauty to be found in Creed’s determination to bring healing to Sylvie. <br /><br />While there is a small plot surrounding Knight’s business, the focus is totally on Creed and Sylvie. Their love conquered the demons and we are given an emotional, heartbreaking yet triumphant love story. From early on you know they are <i>“two halves of one whole.” </i> And while painful to watch, it was such a beautiful thing seeing these two come back to each other. Creed’s Sylvie and Sylvie’s Creed...it couldn't be any other way.<br /><br />The epilogue is right up there among her other greats and the small inclusion of Hawk made my day! <br /><br /><b> “In all the world, there is no heart for me like yours. In all the world, there is no love for you like mine.” ….Mia Angelo</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="11465665858817425497" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1766035812" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer5543022502509042420"><b>*** 3.44 ***<br/><br/>A buddy read with the KA addicts at BB&B! Another week, another macho alpha... :) </b><br/><br/><i>
  <b>"... “Some people get to live life. Some people survive it. We’re survivors. We can carve out our piece of happy, and, I swear to God, baby, right now, you got my vow, for you and for me, the rest of our lives, I’ll bust my ass to carve our piece of happy.”..."</b>
</i><br/><br/>And Sylvie and Creed are two tough survivors! The circumstances of their childhoods were as rough and hostile as they could get, so thank goo</span>
  <span id="freeText5543022502509042420" style="display:none"><b>*** 3.44 ***<br /><br />A buddy read with the KA addicts at BB&amp;B! Another week, another macho alpha... :) </b><br /><br /><i>
  <b>"... “Some people get to live life. Some people survive it. We’re survivors. We can carve out our piece of happy, and, I swear to God, baby, right now, you got my vow, for you and for me, the rest of our lives, I’ll bust my ass to carve our piece of happy.”..."</b>
</i><br /><br />And Sylvie and Creed are two tough survivors! The circumstances of their childhoods were as rough and hostile as they could get, so thank goodness 6 year old Sylvie and her fateful pup were able to meat the 11 year old Creed one evening close to a lake and a pier... He was her Knight is a shining armor then and he was who kept her sane through the years of her growing up, but he was not there to protect her once she became 18 and Sylvie felt betrayed... She did not see him for the next 16 years and by that point had found ways to become a tough, self-reliant, strong woman, who had developed some very unhealthy habits in order to deal with her past... And apart from the heart of gold she has reserved for the few in her circle of friends, Sylvie is low on virtues...<br /><br /><i>
  <b>" ... “I may have mentioned patience wasn't one of my virtues. Actually, I didn't have many virtues but patience definitely wasn't one of them.”..."</b>
</i><br /><br />Ever since he was ran out of town by Sylvie's father, Creed has tried to erase the memory of her from his mind and heart with no success what so ever. He created a life, love and lost since, but she was always the one his soul yearned for. The Sylvie with the smart mouth, habit of bossing and one night stands, a big attitude and a big gun, this Sylvie was not the one he remembered from their youth. But there are the moments when his Sylvie shone through, and he knew she had a hold of his heart just as back in those far away days... And he is willing to be patient and do anything he could possibly do in order to give them another chance. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>" ... “I gave you up once. It killed me. it was figuratively but it still killed me. I’m not doin’ that shit again.”..."</b>
</i><br /><br />Fireworks fly from the moment they meet again and Sylvie is determined to not care about Creed ever again. But this alpha male, gorgeous and gentle, is not giving up and maybe this is what will give her the peace she has craved for a long long time... <br /><br /><i>
  <b>" ... “Just so you know, I speak English. You don’t have to macho-speak with shit like ‘you with me’ after you macho-speak with a bunch of bossing me around. I get you. I’m with you. Or if I’m not, I’ll tell you.”<br />“Noted,” he muttered but sounded like he was smiling.<br />I made the diplomatic decision not to look.”..."</b>
</i><br /><br />Hahaha - I wish more of KA's heroins would say that to their pushy alphas!<br /><br />Overall, it was a pleasant read, but apart from the story of their love, the plot was just so-so... She tends to set us up with drama and we get all prepared for big show-downs, than everything seems to get resolved as an afterthought and you are left a bit cheated by the resolutions... So, not much of a closer here... We got to see Knight and his woman, as well as some positive light on Nick Sebring... KA does follow-up on characters great, almost as great as she writes children!!! And as always, we got a long, very comprehensive Epilogue, which is usually where she gives us the most information and as such are my favorite parts of her books. <br /><br />I wish you all happy reading and a beautiful Fall Weather!!! </span>

    <a title="Jo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14323468-jo"><img alt="Jo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1434090906p2/14323468.jpg" /></a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer919046496" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer44188119708025162"><p>23/09/2016 Buddy read with the KA addicts over at BB&B</p> <p>When Sylvie Bissenette was six and and Tucker Creed was eleven they realised they had something in common, both of them come from broken homes. For eleven years the bond they had blossomed and grew into something so powerful, it was their saving grace, and they were determined to escape their awful homes as soon as Sylvie was old enough. But when the day came, Creed disappeared and Sylvie was forced to live a nightmare. </p> <p>Now it’s sixteen yea</p></span>
  <span id="freeText44188119708025162" style="display:none"><p>23/09/2016 Buddy read with the KA addicts over at BB&amp;B</p> <p>When Sylvie Bissenette was six and and Tucker Creed was eleven they realised they had something in common, both of them come from broken homes. For eleven years the bond they had blossomed and grew into something so powerful, it was their saving grace, and they were determined to escape their awful homes as soon as Sylvie was old enough. But when the day came, Creed disappeared and Sylvie was forced to live a nightmare. </p> <p>Now it’s sixteen years later, and the Sylvie Creed knew is gone, entombed behind a shell so hard, no one can break through. But nothing will stop Creed from getting back Sylvie, his Sylvie that he thought was lost to him forever. </p> <blockquote>
  <i>Tucker Creed. My first love, my protector, my savior.<br />My betrayer.</i>
</blockquote> <p>I really liked Sylvie. After what happened to her, she decided to protect women who were in the same position as she had been, and I respect the hell out of her for that. She’s tough and loyal, and so protective of the few people she cares about. </p> <blockquote>
  <i> “I’m not what you want, Sylvie, I get that because it’s the same for you as it is for me. I’m not what you want ‘cause I’m what you need.” </i>
</blockquote> <p>I did like Creed and how much he loved Sylvie. He was also a great dad to his kids. </p> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “Born to love you, baby,” he repeated. “Die lovin’ you, my Sylvie.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <p>I have to be honest, I didn’t expect to like the romance. Second-chance romances rarely work for me, but in this book the reason why they were apart was heartbreaking. Because of evil men and a love that would do anything to protect, Sylvie and Creed spent sixteen years apart, surviving and not really living. Their past was sad but also beautiful. I liked how KA slowly revealed it to us, how much they loved each other and how much it broke them to lose it. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I did not like the fact that he gave his kids the names Sylvie chose for their kids. I know it was supposed to be romantic, and he had his reasons for doing that, but that just wasn’t okay with me. And the fact that minutes after she found out about this she had sex with him was just all kinds of wrong. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> The sexy times were very hot and I did love that these two finally got the future they planned so many years ago. </p> <blockquote>
  <i> “Got a lot to be thankful for,” he told his window, his words confusing me. “A good woman, beautiful daughter, work I believe in, money, men around me I trust.” He turned back to me. “Still, you left, that hole will not be filled. Not ever.” </i>
</blockquote> <p>My favorite part of this book was Knight, he was fantastic! I liked him in his book, but here I LOVED him!! </p> <p>I’m not a fan of second chance romances. It’s very rare that I will love one. And although I didn’t love this book, I did still enjoy it. But I am tired of second-chance romances where the hero married someone else during the separation from the heroine, had kids, got divorced while the heroine just survives. And I really wished this one had been different. Still, this is KA and I love her books. No other author makes me feel so many emotions while reading a book, and I love that. A must read for all Kristen Ashley (KA) fans.</p></span>
  <a data-text-id="44188119708025162" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/328142178?book_show_action=true">May 11, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mariann {at} Belle&#39;s Book Bag" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mariann {at} Belle&#39;s Book Bag" href="/user/show/6204723-mariann-at-belle-s-book-bag">Mariann {at} Belle&#39;s Book Bag</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6204723-mariann-at-belle-s-book-bag?shelf=my-favorites">my-favorites</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer328142178" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6183306939640187630">Saying that I am a HUGE fan of Kristen Ashley does not even come close to the way I feel about her writing!! Every freaking book of hers has blown me away and left me wanting more!! Sure, there are Kristen Ashley stories that I like more than others, but that is based solely on the characters!! I am definitely addicted and I hope that I continue to be.<br/>I think it is a true sign of how AWESOME a writer is when you can continue to reread their books and it is like reading them for the first time an</span>
  <span id="freeText6183306939640187630" style="display:none">Saying that I am a HUGE fan of Kristen Ashley does not even come close to the way I feel about her writing!! Every freaking book of hers has blown me away and left me wanting more!! Sure, there are Kristen Ashley stories that I like more than others, but that is based solely on the characters!! I am definitely addicted and I hope that I continue to be.<br />I think it is a true sign of how AWESOME a writer is when you can continue to reread their books and it is like reading them for the first time and this always happens for me with her books. Kristen Ashley has a way of writing her characters unlike anything I have ever read. Her strong, loving, arrogant, possessive, dirty~talking ALPHA males suck me(hehe!!)into the stories along with their usually kick~ass, sweet, loving, funny females on the way to their HEA. And I am so happy to say that Creed is no different. <br />OMG...Creed hit me with such an emotional punch that it had my heart aching through the journey between Sylvie and Creed's past and present. I LOVED Sylvie immediately and of course of I LOVED Knight but I was nervous about Creed. I should have known better, Kristen has a way of totally making you hate the hero and then has the ability to make you fall totally head-over-heels in love with him. And, for me, this continued with Creed. He definitely is one of my favorites heroes of hers. Just absolutely loved him!!! *sigh* The necklaces, the tat, his kid's names, and his dirty~talkin mouth. *sigh* Knight had some great moments and I just loved seeing him again!! And then there was Sylvie. Definitely my favorite heroine of hers. She was kick~ass but she was also sweet, caring, loving, and funny. Loved her!! Such tortured souls that I needed desperately to have their HEA together. Kristen just knocked me out with Sylvie and Creed and their story stayed with me long after I was finished. <br />I was on an emotional roller coaster with this book and I was worn out by the end!! But, oh, how I didn't want it to end!! I loved seeing Sylvie and Creed in the past, but I was biting my nails as Sylvie grew closer and closer to her 18th birthday!! BEST EPILOGUE EVER!!*sigh*<br />I can never get enough of Kristen Ashley's writing and I cannot wait for Raid's book next!! Thank you, Kristen, for another book that took me to a world that I didn't want to leave and can't wait to return to!! Creed absolutely has a place in my keeper pile, right next to Knight, to be reread. BEST OF THE BEST rating. <br /><br /><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8981448004252653424"><b>reread with my girls at <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148164-buddies-books-and-baubles' rel='nofollow noopener'>Buddies Books and Baubles</a></b><br/><br/>2nd Read October 2016<br/><br/>Still about a 3.5 star rating. Sophie and Creeds lost years and love story still resonate with me and I was glad to see a heroine suffering in a real way from PTSD and her sexual abuse. Not all girls just shut their legs and let no one in. Some go far in the other direction and use sex as a weapon almost. Great look into how people cope with trauma differently.<br/><br/>1st read Sept 2014:<br/><br/>Sleep? Who needs sleep? I started this thinking </span>
  <span id="freeText8981448004252653424" style="display:none"><b>reread with my girls at <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148164-buddies-books-and-baubles" rel="nofollow noopener">Buddies Books and Baubles</a></b><br /><br />2nd Read October 2016<br /><br />Still about a 3.5 star rating. Sophie and Creeds lost years and love story still resonate with me and I was glad to see a heroine suffering in a real way from PTSD and her sexual abuse. Not all girls just shut their legs and let no one in. Some go far in the other direction and use sex as a weapon almost. Great look into how people cope with trauma differently.<br /><br />1st read Sept 2014:<br /><br />Sleep? Who needs sleep? I started this thinking I’d just get a few chapters in and then go to bed but that never seems to be the case with KA books. There is something about the characters that draws me in and I just can’t let it go until I’m done.<br /><br />This series isn’t for everyone for a number of reasons. The heroes are more anti-heroes teetering on the line between good and bad. Their jobs and tactics might be a bit questionable. There is also something a little guttural or less polished about the words they use, almost caveman like grunting at times. And still I love them, although I’m not sure why. Then there is sex, sex and more sex a lot more than in Knight. I’m not complaining, because it was hot, just warning. <br /><br />Sylvia was a bad ass at work and I was hoping that was going to translate over into her emotional life as well but with Creed she turns into an absolute softy. It is hard to reconcile the two ways she behaves into one person at times for me. <br /><br />I really like the switch back and forth between when they were kids leading up to when everything went wrong and their present lives. I <b>wanted</b> it all to work out, I <b>needed</b> to know what happened that separated them for 16 years. The reconnection of Creed to Sylvie was warm, tender and moving.<br /><br />Other things I enjoyed were seeing Anya and Knight again with their kids as well as a few other characters from the first book. I did like Knight a little bit better but just because it streamlined really well and this might have jumped around too much.<br /><br />If you like KA books then this one will probably be another win for you are well. <br /></span>

  <span id="freeText9515005055072186261" style="display:none">*Slight Spoilers*<br /><br />Ya know, I've said this once...no no no...said this too many times...READ THIS CHICA'S STORIES!! You will NOT be disappointed. This one will go down as one of the greats from her. You get a bit of everything in Creed. The story goes back to present and past. The past put a smile to my face but then again it was heartbreaking.<br /><br />Fucking hot badass mofo. Check.<br />Fucking hot badass chica. Check.<br />Great storyline that leaves ya breathless, heartbroken, teary eyed, laughing and leaves a huge ass smile on your face...Check(to the millionth power).<br /><br />I L-O-V-E stories where the H and H have known each other since they were kids and that they grew up loving one another. And when sucky ass people do things to make them lose one another but then kick ass people bring em back together. The sex, holy balls of fire, verra verra hot and oh so so so fucking sweet. Plus, oh yes there is a huge ass plus, cause MY man Cabe "Hawk" Delgado comes into the story. That made my heart a flutter. Can't say too much so I'll leave with some of my favorite moments/lines:<br /><br /><i>"I'm not what you want, Sylvie, I get that because it's the same for you as it is for me. I'm not what you want 'cause I'm what you need."<br /><br />"Ride 'em, cowgirl," he murmured and it was the first time in my life I came while smiling.<br /><br />"I like morning sex," I warned into the dark. "Fuck me," he muttered. "That's what I'm saying."<br /><br />"My Sylvie."<br /><br />God, I loved it when he watched. </i><p>*Me...THUD*<br /><br /><i>"You know, the rulebook states anything agreed through sexual manipulation is thrown out after the act." "Yeah, if you're makin' love with a normal guy. If you're doin' it with a badass, it's a totally different rulebook." I had to admit, this was true.<br /><br />"My Sylvie, the dreamweaver, makin' dreams come true."<br /><br />"You gonna make me have a spontaneous orgasm at the front door or are you gonna let me get lost in Phoenix?"<br /><br />"I'll never let you go but I'll let you leave...for now."<br /><br />"You're my world, Sylvie. Always have been. Always will be."<br /><br />I looked to cargo pants, boots, skintight Under Armour wearing, dark haired, itense black eyed, hot guy commando Hawk Delgado, got a load of his two phenomenal dimples...</i></p><p>*Me...FUCKING HELL I LOVE HAWK!!!*<br /><br /><i>"Bottom of my soul!" "Bottom of mine."....</i></p><p>Me...*tears*<br /><br /><i>"...Nothing latches onto one of my breasts except your lips." "Now she's making me hard while I'm breaking and entering," Creed griped.<i><br /><br /></i></i></p><p>Epilogue, as always is a killer! Loved how it ended where their love began.</p></span>
  <a data-text-id="9515005055072186261" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_371890848" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/371890848" />
    <a title="Wminbc" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2202962-wminbc"><img alt="Wminbc" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1375905336p2/2202962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/371890848?book_show_action=true">Jul 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wminbc" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wminbc" href="/user/show/2202962-wminbc">Wminbc</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer371890848" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3546638008675116209">As a qualifier...I have NEVER re-read this story. I still, even now nearly 4 years later, hate Creed. I hate what he did to Sylvie even more now than I did in 2012. I have not forgiven him and I don't believe I ever will...I have re-read Knight numerous times, and Sweet Dreams going on 12 times...but this one...never.<br/><br/>Love and devotion…what do those two words really mean. Throughout the story characters ask, "Do you know what love is?" Time and time again there are examples of love. Love is patie</span>
  <span id="freeText3546638008675116209" style="display:none">As a qualifier...I have NEVER re-read this story. I still, even now nearly 4 years later, hate Creed. I hate what he did to Sylvie even more now than I did in 2012. I have not forgiven him and I don't believe I ever will...I have re-read Knight numerous times, and Sweet Dreams going on 12 times...but this one...never.<br /><br />Love and devotion…what do those two words really mean. Throughout the story characters ask, "Do you know what love is?" Time and time again there are examples of love. Love is patient, love is kind, love does not boast or gloat, love need not be two sided, love is never jealous, love is always healing…<br /><br />Devotion, like love, is wonderfully examplified within this story. Knight with Sylvie, Sylvie with the girls, Rhas with Pip, Live with Knight…on and on…but (and READ a HUGE BUT here) just because you tattoo someone's name on your body does not mean you are devoted to them. The symbolism of it being on the back all the more points to the secure knowledge that the person named on your back…Has your back, but does not speak to whether or not you have their back!<br /><br />This was my critique with Creed. I went from being pissed off at him, to furious wishing to cause bodily harm, to utterly and completely disappointed in him. Not to give any spoilers, but the reader needs to decide for themselves how much they could take…and my cudos to Sylvie, because she could take a lot more than I ever could. But, then…she truly loved Creed. <br /><br />Creed, I still firmly do not believe that he loves Sylvie the same way she loves him. If he truly did, he would never, could never have married another woman and given her babies. His selfishness after said babies arrived were all man being man (so no point on dwelling on the kids). But seriously, if he truly loved Sylvie, he would have become a player, messed around, maybe even spend more than one night with a few of them…but he never would have married some one other than his "it". That off my chest, I do believe that Creed believes he loves Sylvie. And, Sylvie believes it now. And, he will be thinking and dreaming of Sylvie while he is with her, so all good.<br /><br />The story was a GREAT story…don't get me wrong. I loved Sylvie and the story and the weave that Ms Ashley wove…I just really hated Creed for most of the story. I was really disappointed that he didn't go back to salt his own wounded heart and get photos or proof that Sylvie was happier without him. That would have shown his love…selfless, giving, generous love would have done that and would have discovered the wasteland that was Sylvie's life. Personally, I would rather be alone than ever settle. I would never give my body or my heart away to someone unless I truly believed they were it. Maybe that is my issue. "For You" had me just as passionate. The reason is the same. Once you have had perfection, a place where your soul knows peace...how could you ever even want to be happy again? Yes, Sylvie forgave him...doesn't mean I have to...Loved the book and loved feeling all those jumbles for Sylvie and for Creed.<br /><br />It is only a great book that can evoke that kind of passion and devotion from the reader! I love Sylvie, I've got her back and if she needs me as a dula or lacation consultant, I am there babe! Love the Epilogue (of course)...but also, I would want to drive too...that irked me too! LOL<br /><br />Reviewed (passionately) by Me</span>
  <a data-text-id="3546638008675116209" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('IJI0VmoArDa6GObDA0k1aU8/v9EauPa/RMJzci2bJU61EhyVvLCLqE4VmDAYxtEi5YiC+zCIBaMXQ/0ZuUGZcQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('odwfZxa0dBWOyoQD/Mfw/wh++Soy/Aa6O4WOFXGmR9o0XDekwARTi3rH+vDnSBS0osnEABjM9aZoBAB+5Xz75Q==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText4357847154026950497" style="display:none">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br /><br />Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends and family around the globe. Her posse is loopy (to say the least) but loopy is good when you want to write.<br /><br />Kristen was raised in a house with a large and multi-generational family. They lived on a very small farm in a small town in the heartland and existed amongst the strains of Glenn Miller, The Everly Brothers, REO Speedwagon and Whitesnake (and the wardrobes that matched).<br /><br />Needless to say, growing up in a house full of music, clothes and love was a good way to grow up. <br /><br />And as she keeps growing up, it keeps getting better.</span>
